msg:This trip was to meet an old friend at Baizhang Temple. Because I couldn't stay in the temple with my child, I found this hotel nearby (don't mislead everyone, the drive is about 50 minutes, not close). Here are the official comments on this opportunity:
1. Location: If you don't drive, it's not very convenient, but it's located in the mountains, with excellent scenery and air (but it's the kind of place with beautiful mountains and waters, but it's boring. We spent half a day sitting and drinking tea and dazed). You can only eat at farmers' houses around, and you have to drive out, which is really unchanged.
2. Room: We booked a suite with two floors. The room is large and generally good, but it doesn't match the price (the price is high).
3. Service: It can only be said to be unsatisfactory. Maybe the hotel is trying hard, but it's really... Maybe I haven't seen a good one, and I always feel awkward.
4. Public facilities: Although there are hot springs and parent-child facilities, they are really bad. Both hot springs and parent-child facilities are "extremely bad", and I even think they are not worthy of the name of parent-child hotel and hot spring hotel.

msg:Every winter, I have to find a place to enjoy a relaxing soak in the hot spring. From Lushan Mountain to Mingyue Mountain and then to Xihai, I have traveled all over Jiangxi's beautiful mountains and waters. This year's first snow is amazing. It is a good choice to take advantage of the baby's suspension of classes to find a warm place to travel during off-peak hours, so the trip to Jiuxian is a natural choice. Starting from Nanchang, the green road is all the way, and the snow scenery along the way is beautiful. It takes about an hour and fifty minutes to reach the hotel. The surrounding environment is elegant, Baizhang Mountain stands tall, and the stream flows. The hotel is also very a**ospheric, the equipment is very new, the front desk is very enthusiastic, check-in is quick, and the room type is upgraded for free, nice! The room has a hot spring on one side and Baizhang Mountain on the other side. You can directly enjoy the snow scenery. The facilities in the room are very complete, and each tea cup is individually sealed and disinfected. This is the first time we have encountered so many hotels we have stayed in. It is really detailed. Of course, the biggest feature of the hotel is undoubtedly parent-child. A whole floor of parent-child park is very competitive even in Nanchang, not to mention various parent-child activities, which is really amazing! By the way, it feels great to book the venue during off-peak hours. You can see the picture. The biggest surprise was that I could enjoy unlimited hot springs for two days after staying for one night. I really didn't expect such a good thing. After checking out, I enjoyed the warmth for an extra afternoon. It was really cost-effective! Highly recommended!
